function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 75') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.75!');
}

	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: plugins/system/000_registration/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html') && (sha1_file('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/system/000_registration/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/system/000_registration/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/system/000_registration/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/system/000_registration/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/system/000_registration/index.html');
}

			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '40372e260079cf5ec58addb654927454088e19cb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') != '2bd89ba9599ef4a26f26e7c89ff8bcf98f8415d3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') !== '2bd89ba9599ef4a26f26e7c89ff8bcf98f8415d3') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') !== '6512c7a2d7e0ba2ece100e2baadc3ccb987618b0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php') !== '2bd89ba9599ef4a26f26e7c89ff8bcf98f8415d3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/102_change_email/plugin.inc.php');
		}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.js');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.js') != '2b978000a0c36f26f0ec6426e24de6f3e94c6c05') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '2b978000a0c36f26f0ec6426e24de6f3e94c6c05') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '5182ca1b52006556f580d7e99876f469bd374cc3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '2b978000a0c36f26f0ec6426e24de6f3e94c6c05') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 76\n");
